363 -> metal/formaldehyde-sensitive transcriptional repressor -> "Proteins that bind to both copper, nickel or cobalt ions via conserved cysteine and histidine residues and to promoter regions to repress transcription. When bound to metal ions they are unable to bind DNA, leading to transcriptional derepression. Not likely to be related to antibacterial resistance."
